<s> of the two manuscripts mrs <\s>
<s> shelley's transcript is the later and more authoritative 1 <\s>
<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>
<s> our purses are empty our swords are cold give us glory and blood and gold <\s>
<s> lawyers and priests a motley crowd to the earth their pale brows bowed like a bad prayer not over loud whispering 'thou art law and god 18 <\s>
<s> then all cried with one accord 70 thou art king and god and lord anarchy to thee we bow be thy name made holy now <\s>
<s> and anarchy the skeleton bowed and grinned to every one 75 as well as if his education had cost ten millions to the nation <\s>
<s> for he knew the palaces of our kings were rightly his his the sceptre crown and globe 80 and the gold inwoven robe <\s>
<s> so he sent his slaves before to seize upon the bank and tower and was proceeding with intent to meet his pensioned parliament 85 22 <\s>
<s> when one fled past a maniac maid and her name was hope she said but she looked more like despair and she cried out in the air 23 <\s>
<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>
<s> when between her and her foes a mist a light an image rose small at first and weak and frail like the vapour of a vale 105 27 <\s>
<s> till as clouds grow on the blast like tower crowned giants striding fast and glare with lightnings as they fly and speak in thunder to the sky 28 <\s>
<s> it grew a shape arrayed in mail 110 brighter than the viper's scale and upborne on wings whose grain was as the light of sunny rain <\s>
<s> on its helm seen far away a planet like the morning's lay 115 and those plumes its light rained through like a shower of crimson dew <\s>
<s> with step as soft as wind it passed o'er the heads of men so fast that they knew the presence there 120 and looked but all was empty air <\s>
<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>
<s> birds find rest in narrow nest when weary of their winged quest beasts find fare in woody lair when storm and snow are in the air <\s>
<s> asses swine have litter spread and with fitting food are fed all things have a home but one thou oh englishman hast none <\s>
<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>
<s> what art thou freedom <\s>
<s> could slaves answer from their living graves 210 this demand tyrants would flee like a dream's dim imagery 53 <\s>
<s> thou art not as impostors say a shadow soon to pass away a superstition and a name 215 echoing from the cave of fame <\s>
<s> for the labourer thou art bread and a comely table spread from his daily labour come in a neat and happy home <\s>
<s> thou art clothes and fire and food for the trampled multitude no in countries that are free such starvation cannot be as in england now we see <\s>
<s> to the rich thou art a check when his foot is on the neck of his victim thou dost make that he treads upon a snake <\s>
<s> thou art justice ne'er for gold 230 may thy righteous laws be sold as laws are in england thou shield'st alike the high and low <\s>
<s> thou art wisdom freemen never dream that god will damn for ever 235 all who think those things untrue of which priests make such ado <\s>
<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>
<s> birds find rest in narrow nest when weary of their winged quest beasts find fare in woody lair when storm and snow are in the air <\s>
<s> asses swine have litter spread and with fitting food are fed all things have a home but one thou oh englishman hast none <\s>
<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>
<s> what art thou freedom <\s>
<s> could slaves answer from their living graves 210 this demand tyrants would flee like a dream's dim imagery 53 <\s>
<s> thou art not as impostors say a shadow soon to pass away a superstition and a name 215 echoing from the cave of fame <\s>
<s> for the labourer thou art bread and a comely table spread from his daily labour come in a neat and happy home <\s>
<s> thou art clothes and fire and food for the trampled multitude no in countries that are free such starvation cannot be as in england now we see <\s>
<s> to the rich thou art a check when his foot is on the neck of his victim thou dost make that he treads upon a snake <\s>
<s> thou art justice ne'er for gold 230 may thy righteous laws be sold as laws are in england thou shield'st alike the high and low <\s>
<s> thou art wisdom freemen never dream that god will damn for ever 235 all who think those things untrue of which priests make such ado <\s>
<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>
<s> our purses are empty our swords are cold give us glory and blood and gold <\s>
<s> lawyers and priests a motley crowd to the earth their pale brows bowed like a bad prayer not over loud whispering 'thou art law and god 18 <\s>
<s> then all cried with one accord 70 thou art king and god and lord anarchy to thee we bow be thy name made holy now <\s>
<s> and anarchy the skeleton bowed and grinned to every one 75 as well as if his education had cost ten millions to the nation <\s>
<s> for he knew the palaces of our kings were rightly his his the sceptre crown and globe 80 and the gold inwoven robe <\s>
<s> so he sent his slaves before to seize upon the bank and tower and was proceeding with intent to meet his pensioned parliament 85 22 <\s>
<s> when one fled past a maniac maid and her name was hope she said but she looked more like despair and she cried out in the air 23 <\s>
<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>

<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>
<s> our purses are empty our swords are cold give us glory and blood and gold <\s>
<s> lawyers and priests a motley crowd to the earth their pale brows bowed like a bad prayer not over loud whispering 'thou art law and god 18 <\s>
<s> then all cried with one accord 70 thou art king and god and lord anarchy to thee we bow be thy name made holy now <\s>
<s> and anarchy the skeleton bowed and grinned to every one 75 as well as if his education had cost ten millions to the nation <\s>
<s> for he knew the palaces of our kings were rightly his his the sceptre crown and globe 80 and the gold inwoven robe <\s>
<s> so he sent his slaves before to seize upon the bank and tower and was proceeding with intent to meet his pensioned parliament 85 22 <\s>
<s> when one fled past a maniac maid and her name was hope she said but she looked more like despair and she cried out in the air 23 <\s>
<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>
<s> when between her and her foes a mist a light an image rose small at first and weak and frail like the vapour of a vale 105 27 <\s>
<s> till as clouds grow on the blast like tower crowned giants striding fast and glare with lightnings as they fly and speak in thunder to the sky 28 <\s>
<s> it grew a shape arrayed in mail 110 brighter than the viper's scale and upborne on wings whose grain was as the light of sunny rain <\s>
<s> on its helm seen far away a planet like the morning's lay 115 and those plumes its light rained through like a shower of crimson dew <\s>
<s> with step as soft as wind it passed o'er the heads of men so fast that they knew the presence there 120 and looked but all was empty air <\s>
<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>
<s> birds find rest in narrow nest when weary of their winged quest beasts find fare in woody lair when storm and snow are in the air <\s>
<s> asses swine have litter spread and with fitting food are fed all things have a home but one thou oh englishman hast none <\s>
<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>

<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> of the two manuscripts mrs <\s>
<s> shelley's transcript is the later and more authoritative 1 <\s>
<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>
<s> our purses are empty our swords are cold give us glory and blood and gold <\s>
<s> lawyers and priests a motley crowd to the earth their pale brows bowed like a bad prayer not over loud whispering 'thou art law and god 18 <\s>
<s> then all cried with one accord 70 thou art king and god and lord anarchy to thee we bow be thy name made holy now <\s>
<s> and anarchy the skeleton bowed and grinned to every one 75 as well as if his education had cost ten millions to the nation <\s>
<s> for he knew the palaces of our kings were rightly his his the sceptre crown and globe 80 and the gold inwoven robe <\s>
<s> so he sent his slaves before to seize upon the bank and tower and was proceeding with intent to meet his pensioned parliament 85 22 <\s>
<s> when one fled past a maniac maid and her name was hope she said but she looked more like despair and she cried out in the air 23 <\s>
<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>
<s> when between her and her foes a mist a light an image rose small at first and weak and frail like the vapour of a vale 105 27 <\s>
<s> till as clouds grow on the blast like tower crowned giants striding fast and glare with lightnings as they fly and speak in thunder to the sky 28 <\s>
<s> it grew a shape arrayed in mail 110 brighter than the viper's scale and upborne on wings whose grain was as the light of sunny rain <\s>
<s> on its helm seen far away a planet like the morning's lay 115 and those plumes its light rained through like a shower of crimson dew <\s>
<s> with step as soft as wind it passed o'er the heads of men so fast that they knew the presence there 120 and looked but all was empty air <\s>
<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>
<s> birds find rest in narrow nest when weary of their winged quest beasts find fare in woody lair when storm and snow are in the air <\s>
<s> asses swine have litter spread and with fitting food are fed all things have a home but one thou oh englishman hast none <\s>
<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>
<s> what art thou freedom <\s>
<s> could slaves answer from their living graves 210 this demand tyrants would flee like a dream's dim imagery 53 <\s>
<s> thou art not as impostors say a shadow soon to pass away a superstition and a name 215 echoing from the cave of fame <\s>
<s> for the labourer thou art bread and a comely table spread from his daily labour come in a neat and happy home <\s>
<s> thou art clothes and fire and food for the trampled multitude no in countries that are free such starvation cannot be as in england now we see <\s>
<s> to the rich thou art a check when his foot is on the neck of his victim thou dost make that he treads upon a snake <\s>
<s> thou art justice ne'er for gold 230 may thy righteous laws be sold as laws are in england thou shield'st alike the high and low <\s>
<s> thou art wisdom freemen never dream that god will damn for ever 235 all who think those things untrue of which priests make such ado <\s>
<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>

<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>
<s> when between her and her foes a mist a light an image rose small at first and weak and frail like the vapour of a vale 105 27 <\s>
<s> till as clouds grow on the blast like tower crowned giants striding fast and glare with lightnings as they fly and speak in thunder to the sky 28 <\s>
<s> it grew a shape arrayed in mail 110 brighter than the viper's scale and upborne on wings whose grain was as the light of sunny rain <\s>
<s> on its helm seen far away a planet like the morning's lay 115 and those plumes its light rained through like a shower of crimson dew <\s>
<s> with step as soft as wind it passed o'er the heads of men so fast that they knew the presence there 120 and looked but all was empty air <\s>
<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>
<s> birds find rest in narrow nest when weary of their winged quest beasts find fare in woody lair when storm and snow are in the air <\s>
<s> asses swine have litter spread and with fitting food are fed all things have a home but one thou oh englishman hast none <\s>
<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>
<s> what art thou freedom <\s>
<s> could slaves answer from their living graves 210 this demand tyrants would flee like a dream's dim imagery 53 <\s>
<s> thou art not as impostors say a shadow soon to pass away a superstition and a name 215 echoing from the cave of fame <\s>
<s> for the labourer thou art bread and a comely table spread from his daily labour come in a neat and happy home <\s>
<s> thou art clothes and fire and food for the trampled multitude no in countries that are free such starvation cannot be as in england now we see <\s>
<s> to the rich thou art a check when his foot is on the neck of his victim thou dost make that he treads upon a snake <\s>
<s> thou art justice ne'er for gold 230 may thy righteous laws be sold as laws are in england thou shield'st alike the high and low <\s>
<s> thou art wisdom freemen never dream that god will damn for ever 235 all who think those things untrue of which priests make such ado <\s>
<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>

<s> this is slavery savage men 205 or wild beasts within a den would endure not as ye do but such ills they never knew <\s>
<s> what art thou freedom <\s>
<s> could slaves answer from their living graves 210 this demand tyrants would flee like a dream's dim imagery 53 <\s>
<s> thou art not as impostors say a shadow soon to pass away a superstition and a name 215 echoing from the cave of fame <\s>
<s> for the labourer thou art bread and a comely table spread from his daily labour come in a neat and happy home <\s>
<s> thou art clothes and fire and food for the trampled multitude no in countries that are free such starvation cannot be as in england now we see <\s>
<s> to the rich thou art a check when his foot is on the neck of his victim thou dost make that he treads upon a snake <\s>
<s> thou art justice ne'er for gold 230 may thy righteous laws be sold as laws are in england thou shield'st alike the high and low <\s>
<s> thou art wisdom freemen never dream that god will damn for ever 235 all who think those things untrue of which priests make such ado <\s>
<s> thou art peace never by thee would blood and treasure wasted be as tyrants wasted them when all 240 leagued to quench thy flame in gaul <\s>
<s> what if english toil and blood was poured forth even as a flood <\s>
<s> it availed oh liberty to dim but not extinguish thee <\s>
<s> thou art love the rich have kissed thy feet and like him following christ give their substance to the free and through the rough world follow thee 62 <\s>
<s> or turn their wealth to arms and make 250 war for thy beloved sake on wealth and war and fraud whence they drew the power which is their prey <\s>
<s> science poetry and thought are thy lamps they make the lot 255 of the dwellers in a cot so serene they curse it not <\s>
<s> spirit patience gentleness all that can adorn and bless art thou let deeds not words express 260 thine exceeding loveliness <\s>
<s> let a great assembly be of the fearless and the free on some spot of english ground where the plains stretch wide around <\s>
<s> let the blue sky overhead the green earth on which ye tread all that must eternal be witness the solemnity <\s>
<s> from the corners uttermost 270 of the bounds of english coast from every hut village and town where those who live and suffer moan for others misery or their own 68 <\s>
<s> from the workhouse and the prison where pale as corpses newly risen women children young and old 277 groan for pain and weep for cold 69 <\s>
<s> from the haunts of daily life where is waged the daily strife 280 with common wants and common cares which sows the human heart with tares 70 <\s>
<s> lastly from the palaces where the murmur of distress echoes like the distant sound 285 of a wind alive around 71 <\s>
<s> those prison halls of wealth and fashion where some few feel such compassion for those who groan and toil and wail as must make their brethren pale 72 <\s>
<s> ye who suffer woes untold 291 or to feel or to behold your lost country bought and sold with a price of blood and gold 73 <\s>
<s> let a vast assembly be 295 and with great solemnity declare with measured words that ye are as god has made ye free 74 <\s>
<s> be your strong and simple words keen to wound as sharpened swords 300 and wide as targes let them be with their shade to cover ye <\s>
<s> let the tyrants pour around with a quick and startling sound like the loosening of a sea 305 troops of armed emblazonry <\s>
<s> let the charged artillery drive till the dead air seems alive with the clash of clanging wheels and the tramp of horses heels <\s>
<s> let the fixed bayonet gleam with sharp desire to wet its bright point in english blood looking keen as one for food <\s>
<s> let the horsemen's scimitars 315 wheel and flash like sphereless stars thirsting to eclipse their burning in a sea of death and mourning <\s>
<s> stand ye calm and resolute like a forest close and mute 320 with folded arms and looks which are weapons of unvanquished war 80 <\s>
<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>

<s> as i lay asleep in italy there came a voice from over the sea and with great power it forth led me to walk in the visions of poesy <\s>
<s> i met murder on the way 5 he had a mask like castlereagh very smooth he looked yet grim seven blood hounds followed him 3 <\s>
<s> all were fat and well they might be in admirable plight 10 for one by one and two by two he tossed them human hearts to chew which from his wide cloak he drew <\s>
<s> next came fraud and he had on like eldon an ermined gown 15 his big tears for he wept well turned to mill stones as they fell <\s>
<s> and the little children who round his feet played to and fro thinking every tear a gem 20 had their brains knocked out by them <\s>
<s> clothed with the bible as with light and the shadows of the night like sidmouth next hypocrisy on a crocodile rode by <\s>
<s> and many more destructions played in this ghastly masquerade all disguised even to the eyes like bishops lawyers peers or spies <\s>
<s> last came anarchy he rode 30 on a white horse splashed with blood he was pale even to the lips like death in the apocalypse <\s>
<s> and he wore a kingly crown and in his grasp a sceptre shone 35 on his brow this mark i saw i am god and king and law <\s>
<s> with a pace stately and fast over english land he passed trampling to a mire of blood 40 the adoring multitude <\s>
<s> and a mighty troop around with their trampling shook the ground waving each a bloody sword for the service of their lord <\s>
<s> and with glorious triumph they rode through england proud and gay drunk as with intoxication of the wine of desolation <\s>
<s> o'er fields and towns from sea to sea 50 passed the pageant swift and free tearing up and trampling down till they came to london town <\s>
<s> and each dweller panic stricken felt his heart with terror sicken 55 hearing the tempestuous cry of the triumph of anarchy <\s>
<s> for with pomp to meet him came clothed in arms like blood and flame the hired murderers who did sing 60 thou art god and law and king <\s>
<s> we have waited weak and lone for thy coming mighty one <\s>
<s> our purses are empty our swords are cold give us glory and blood and gold <\s>
<s> lawyers and priests a motley crowd to the earth their pale brows bowed like a bad prayer not over loud whispering 'thou art law and god 18 <\s>
<s> then all cried with one accord 70 thou art king and god and lord anarchy to thee we bow be thy name made holy now <\s>
<s> and anarchy the skeleton bowed and grinned to every one 75 as well as if his education had cost ten millions to the nation <\s>
<s> for he knew the palaces of our kings were rightly his his the sceptre crown and globe 80 and the gold inwoven robe <\s>
<s> so he sent his slaves before to seize upon the bank and tower and was proceeding with intent to meet his pensioned parliament 85 22 <\s>
<s> when one fled past a maniac maid and her name was hope she said but she looked more like despair and she cried out in the air 23 <\s>
<s> my father time is weak and gray 90 with waiting for a better day see how idiot like he stands fumbling with his palsied hands <\s>
<s> he has had child after child and the dust of death is piled 95 over every one but me misery oh misery <\s>
<s> then she lay down in the street right before the horses feet expecting with a patient eye 100 murder fraud and anarchy <\s>
<s> when between her and her foes a mist a light an image rose small at first and weak and frail like the vapour of a vale 105 27 <\s>
<s> till as clouds grow on the blast like tower crowned giants striding fast and glare with lightnings as they fly and speak in thunder to the sky 28 <\s>
<s> it grew a shape arrayed in mail 110 brighter than the viper's scale and upborne on wings whose grain was as the light of sunny rain <\s>
<s> on its helm seen far away a planet like the morning's lay 115 and those plumes its light rained through like a shower of crimson dew <\s>
<s> with step as soft as wind it passed o'er the heads of men so fast that they knew the presence there 120 and looked but all was empty air <\s>
<s> as flowers beneath may's footstep waken as stars from night's loose hair are shaken as waves arise when loud winds call thoughts sprung where'er that step did fall <\s>
<s> and the prostrate multitude looked and ankle deep in blood hope that maiden most serene was walking with a quiet mien 33 <\s>
<s> and anarchy the ghastly birth 130 lay dead earth upon the earth the horse of death tameless as wind fled and with his hoofs did grind to dust the murderers thronged behind <\s>
<s> a rushing light of clouds and splendour 135 a sense awakening and yet tender was heard and felt and at its close these words of joy and fear arose 35 <\s>
<s> as if their own indignant earth which gave the sons of england birth 140 had felt their blood upon her brow and shuddering with a mother's throe 36 <\s>
<s> had turned every drop of blood by which her face had been bedewed to an accent unwithstood 145 as if her heart had cried aloud 37 <\s>
<s> men of england heirs of glory heroes of unwritten story nurslings of one mighty mother hopes of her and one another 150 38 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
<s> what is freedom ye can tell that which slavery is too well for its very name has grown to an echo of your own <\s>
<s> tis to work and have such pay 160 as just keeps life from day to day in your limbs as in a cell for the tyrants use to dwell 41 <\s>
<s> so that ye for them are made loom and plough and sword and spade 165 with or without your own will bent to their defence and nourishment <\s>
<s> tis to see your children weak with their mothers pine and peak when the winter winds are bleak 170 they are dying whilst i speak <\s>
<s> tis to hunger for such diet as the rich man in his riot casts to the fat dogs that lie surfeiting beneath his eye 175 44 <\s>
<s> tis to let the ghost of gold take from toil a thousandfold more than e'er its substance could in the tyrannies of old <\s>
<s> paper coin that forgery 180 of the title deeds which ye hold to something of the worth of the inheritance of earth <\s>
<s> tis to be a slave in soul and to hold no strong control 185 over your own wills but be all that others make of ye <\s>
<s> and at length when ye complain with a murmur weak and vain tis to see the tyrant's crew 190 ride over your wives and you blood is on the grass like dew <\s>
<s> then it is to feel revenge fiercely thirsting to exchange blood for blood and wrong for wrong 195 do not thus when ye are strong <\s>

<s> and let panic who outspeeds the career of armed steeds pass a disregarded shade 325 through your phalanx undismayed <\s>
<s> let the laws of your own land good or ill between ye stand hand to hand and foot to foot arbiters of the dispute 330 82 <\s>
<s> the old laws of england they whose reverend heads with age are gray children of a wiser day and whose solemn voice must be thine own echo liberty <\s>
<s> on those who first should violate such sacred heralds in their state rest the blood that must ensue and it will not rest on you <\s>
<s> and if then the tyrants dare 340 let them ride among you there slash and stab and maim and hew what they like that let them do <\s>
<s> with folded arms and steady eyes and little fear and less surprise 345 look upon them as they slay till their rage has died away <\s>
<s> then they will return with shame to the place from which they came and the blood thus shed will speak 350 in hot blushes on their cheek <\s>
<s> every woman in the land will point at them as they stand they will hardly dare to greet their acquaintance in the street <\s>
<s> and the bold true warriors who have hugged danger in wars will turn to those who would be free ashamed of such base company <\s>
<s> and that slaughter to the nation 360 shall steam up like inspiration eloquent oracular a volcano heard afar <\s>
<s> and these words shall then become like oppression's thundered doom 365 ringing through each heart and brain heard again again again 91 <\s>
<s> rise like lions after slumber in unvanquishable number shake your chains to earth like dew 370 which in sleep had fallen on you ye are many they are few <\s>
